    <script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        $("document").ready(function () {
   
            $('#btnSaveNewsletter').click( function() {

                if (!validateFormExtended('#nl-form-1','#newsletterError',false,false))
                    return false;

                $('#newsletterError').hide()
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                    url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Account.svc/NewsletterUserSave",
                    dataType: "json",
                    cache: false,
                    data: '{"Email": "' + $('#newsletterEmail').val() + '","LanguageId": "' + "de" + '","FirstName": "","LastName": ""}',
	 
                    timeout: 50000,
                    success: function (data) 
                    {
                        if (data != null && !data.d.Status.Error) {
                            $('#newsletterEmail').hide();
                            $('#btnSaveNewsletter').hide();
                            $('#newsletterSuccesse').html("Sie haben sich erfolgreich für den Newsletter angemeldet.");
                            $('#newsletterSuccesse').fadeIn(1000);
                        }
                        else {
                            $('#newsletterError').html("Leider ist ein Fehler aufgetreten. Bitte versuchen Sie es nochmals.");
                            $('#newsletterError').fadeIn();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (xhr) 
                    {
                        alert(xhr.responseText);
                        if (xhr.responseText)
                            $('#newsletterError').html(xhr.responseText);
                        $('#newsletterError').fadeIn()
                        return;
                        
                    }
                });
            });

        });

    </script>

        <script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        var valid=true;
        $("document").ready(function () {
            var languageID = "de";
            $("#mainSearchTextField,#mainSearchTextFieldM").autocomplete({
                source: function (request, response) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                        url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Search.svc/AutoCompleteSearchQuery",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: '{"searchString":"' + request.term.replace(/"/g, "\\\"") + '","languageId":"de"}',
                        success: function (obj) {
                            response($.map(obj.d.autoCompleteResult.SuggestedProducts, function (item) {
                                return {
                                    label: item.ProductName, //Suggestions
                                    value: item.ProductName, //InputField
                                    productID: item.ProductId,
                                    notificationID: item.NotificationId
                                }
                            }));
                        },
                        error: function (xhr) {
                            return;
                        }
                    });
                },
                minLength: 2,
                delay: 1000,
                select: function (event, ui) {valid=false;
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                        url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Search.svc/AutoCompleteNotify",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: '{"notificationID":"' + ui.item.notificationID + '"}',
                        success: function (obj) {
                        },
                        error: function (xhr) {
                            if (xhr.responseText) {
                                $("body").html(xhr.responseText);
                            }
                            return;
                        },
                        complete: function () {
                            $.ajax({
                                type: "GET",
                                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                                url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Product.svc/ProductSEOGet?ProductId=" + ui.item.productID + "&LanguageId=" + languageID,
                                dataType: "json",
                                data: {},
                                success: function (obj) {
                                    if (obj.d.ProductSEO == null || obj.d.ProductSEO.length < 1)
                                        alert("product not found");
                                    else
                                        window.location = obj.d.ProductSEO.Url;
                                },
                                error: function (xhr) {
                                    if (xhr.responseText) {
                                        $("body").html(xhr.responseText);
                                    }
                                    return;
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                },
                open: function () {
                    $(this).removeClass("ui-corner-all").removeClass("ui-corner-top");
                },
                close: function () {
                    $(this).removeClass("ui-corner-top").removeClass("ui-corner-all");
                }
            });

           
        });
    </script>
